Req-498:  the sailing termination shall be set to [True]  for at most 26 seconds within at least 10 seconds , when the IDC inhibitor equals [True] , if the engine error is less than the sailing termination within at most 23 seconds , while the NoSailing requests whose index equals 0 is above the IDC inhibitor for 12 seconds  .
[
comp( 
[ 
subComp(act, Nil, Nil, the sailing termination, shall be set, [[True], ], the sailing termination shall be set to [True]),
subComp(v-time, for, at most, 26, seconds, [], for at most 26 seconds),
subComp(pre-time, within, at least, 10, seconds, [], within at least 10 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(ttrig, Nil, when, the IDC inhibitor, equals, [[True], ], when the IDC inhibitor equals [True] )
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the engine error, is less than, [the sailing termination, ], if the engine error is less than the sailing termination ),
subComp(pre-time, within, at most, 23, seconds, [], within at most 23 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(condScope, Nil, while, the NoSailing requests, is above, [the IDC inhibitor, ], while the NoSailing requests is above the IDC inhibitor ),
subComp(hidden, the NoSailing requests, whose, index, equals, [0, ], the NoSailing requests whose index equals 0 ),
subComp(v-time, for, , 12, seconds, [], for 12 seconds)
] )

]

%%%
Req-499: before the LSC is greater than the quality signal ,  the quality signal shall be sent to the sailing termination  for at least 23 seconds , if the quality signal is less than the vehicle speed setpoint , if the quality signal is less than the vehicle speed setpoint  .
[
comp( 
[ 
subComp(condScope, Nil, before, the LSC, is greater than, [the quality signal, ], before the LSC is greater than the quality signal )
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(act, Nil, Nil, the quality signal, shall be sent, [the sailing termination, ], the quality signal shall be sent to the sailing termination),
subComp(v-time, for, at least, 23, seconds, [], for at least 23 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the quality signal, is less than, [the vehicle speed setpoint, ], if the quality signal is less than the vehicle speed setpoint )
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the quality signal, is less than, [the vehicle speed setpoint, ], if the quality signal is less than the vehicle speed setpoint )
] )

]

] ),

[
